callcompile_kernel { "kernel_code": "\nimport torch\nimport torch.nn as nn\nfrom torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline\n\ncpp_sources = \"\"\"\n#include <torch/extension.h>\n\ntorch::Tensor forward_cuda(torch::Tensor x, torch::Tensor w1, torch::Tensor b1, torch::Tensor w2, torch::Tensor b2, torch::Tensor w_ds, torch::Tensor b_ds, int stride);\n\"\"\"\n\ncuda_sources = \"\"\"\n#include <torch/extension.h>\n\n__global__ void __launch_bounds__(256) fused_basic_block_kernel(\n const float* __restrict__ x,\n const float* __restrict__ w1,\n const float* __restrict__ b1,\n const float* __restrict__ w2,\n const float* __restrict__ b2,\n const float* __restrict__ w_ds,\n const float* __restrict__ b_ds,\n float* __restrict__ y,\n int B, int C_in, int H, int W, int C_out, int stride)\n{\n const int TILE = 8;\n const int tile_conv1 = TILE + 2;\n const int tile_in = (tile_conv1 - 1) * stride + 3;\n const int tile_conv1_area = tile_conv1 * tile_conv1;\n\n int bx = blockIdx.x;\n int by = blockIdx.y;\n int bz = blockIdx.z;\n\n int base_out_h = by * TILE;\n int base_out_w = bx * TILE;\n int base_in_h = base_out_h * stride - 1;\n int base_in_w = base_out_w * stride - 1;\n\n int tid = threadIdx.x;\n\n extern __shared__ float sbuf[];\n float* x_shared = sbuf;\n float* w1_shared = x_shared + tile_in * tile_in * C_in;\n float* relu1_shared = w1_shared + C_out * C_in * 9;\n\n // Load x into shared memory\n int total_in = tile_in * tile_in * C_in;\n for (int idx = tid; idx < total_in; idx += blockDim.x) {\n int c = idx % C_in;\n int rem = idx / C_in;\n int w = rem % tile_in;\n int h = rem / tile_in;\n int gh = base_in_h + h;\n int gw = base_in_w + w;\n float val = 0.0f;\n if (gh >= 0 && gh < H && gw >= 0 && gw < W) {\n val = x[((bz * C_in + c) * H + gh) * W + gw];\n }\n x_shared[(h * tile_in + w) * C_in + c] = val;\n }\n\n // Load w1 into shared memory\n int total_w1 = C_out * C_in * 9;\n for (int idx = tid; idx < total_w1; idx += blockDim.x) {\n w1_shared[idx] = w1[idx];\n }\n __syncthreads();\n\n // Compute conv1 + BN + ReLU for the intermediate tile\n int total_conv1 = tile_conv1 * tile_conv1 * C_out;\n for (int idx = tid; idx < total_conv1; idx += blockDim.x) {\n int oc = idx % C_out;\n int pos = idx / C_out;\n int pw = pos % tile_conv1;\n int ph = pos / tile_conv1;\n\n float sum = 0.0f;\n for (int ic = 0; ic < C_in; ic++) {\n #pragma unroll\n for (int dy = -1; dy <= 1; dy++) {\n for (int dx = -1; dx <= 1; dx++) {\n int ix = 1 + pw * stride + dx;\n int iy = 1 + ph * stride + dy;\n float xv = x_shared[(iy * tile_in + ix) * C_in + ic];\n float wv = w1_shared[((oc * C_in + ic) * 3 + (dy + 1)) * 3 + (dx + 1)];\n sum += xv * wv;\n }\n }\n }\n sum = sum + b1[oc];\n if (sum < 0.0f) sum = 0.0f;\n relu1_shared[oc * tile_conv1_area + ph * tile_conv1 + pw] = sum;\n }\n __syncthreads();\n\n // Compute conv2 + downsample + add + ReLU for output positions\n int H_out = (H - 1) / stride + 1;\n int W_out = (W - 1) / stride + 1;\n\n int lane_id = tid & 31;\n int warp_id = tid >> 5;\n int channel_group = warp_id >> 1;\n int spatial_base = (warp_id & 1) << 5;\n int spatial_idx = spatial_base | lane_id;\n\n int tx = spatial_idx % TILE;\n int ty = spatial_idx / TILE;\n int out_h = base_out_h + ty;\n int out_w = base_out_w + tx;\n\n if (spatial_idx < TILE * TILE && out_h < H_out && out_w < W_out) {\n int channels_per_group = (C_out + 3) / 4;\n int oc_start = channel_group * channels_per_group;\n int oc_end = min(oc_start + channels_per_group, C_out);\n\n for (int oc = oc_start; oc < oc_end; ++oc) {\n // conv2\n float sum = 0.0f;\n for (int ic = 0; ic < C_out; ic++) {\n int relu1_base = ic * tile_conv1_area;\n #pragma unroll\n for (int dy = -1; dy <= 1; dy++) {\n int c1y = ty + 1 + dy;\n for (int dx = -1; dx <= 1; dx++) {\n int c1x = tx + 1 + dx;\n float v = relu1_shared[relu1_base + c1y * tile_conv1 + c1x];\n float w = w2[((oc * C_out + ic) * 3 + (dy + 1)) * 3 + (dx + 1)];\n sum += v * w;\n }\n }\n }\n sum = sum + b2[oc];\n\n // downsample\n float ds_val = 0.0f;\n int xh = out_h * stride;\n int xw = out_w * stride;\n for (int ic = 0; ic < C_in; ic++) {\n ds_val += x[((bz * C_in + ic) * H + xh) * W + xw] * w_ds[oc * C_in + ic];\n }\n ds_val = ds_val + b_ds[oc];\n\n float res = sum + ds_val;\n if (res < 0.0f) res = 0.0f;\n\n y[((bz * C_out + oc) * H_out + out_h) * W_out + out_w] = res;\n }\n }\n}\n\ntorch::Tensor forward_cuda(\n torch::Tensor x,\n torch::Tensor w1, torch::Tensor b1,\n torch::Tensor w2, torch::Tensor b2,\n torch::Tensor w_ds, torch::Tensor b_ds,\n int stride)\n{\n int B = x.size(0);\n int C_in = x.size(1);\n int H = x.size(2);\n int W = x.size(3);\n int C_out = w1.size(0);\n\n int H_out = (H - 1) / stride + 1;\n int W_out = (W - 1) / stride + 1;\n\n auto y = torch::empty({B, C_out, H_out, W_out}, x.options());\n\n const int TILE = 8;\n dim3 block(256);\n dim3 grid((W_out + TILE - 1) / TILE, (H_out + TILE - 1) / stride + 1;\n int W_out = (W - 1) / stride + 1;\n\n int lane_id = tid & 31;\n int warp_id = tid >> 5;\n int channel_group = warp_id >> 1;\n int spatial_base = (warp_id & 1) << 5;\n int spatial_idx = spatial_base | lane_id;\n\n int tx = spatial_idx % TILE;\n int ty = spatial_idx / TILE;\n int out_h = base_out_h + ty;\n int out_w = base_out_w + tx;\n\n if (spatial_idx < TILE * TILE && out_h < H_out && out_w < W_out) {\n int channels_per_group = (C_out + 3) / 4;\n int oc_start = channel_group * channels_per_group;\n int oc_end = min(oc_start + channels_per_group, C_out);\n\n for (int oc = oc_start; oc < oc_end; ++oc) {\n float sum = 0.0f;\n for (int ic = 0; ic < C_out; ic++) {\n int relu1_base = ic * tile_conv1_area;\n for (int dy = -1; dy <= 1; dy++) {\n int c1y = ty + 1 + dy;\n for (int dx = -1; dx <= 1; dx++) {\n int c1x = tx + 1 + dx;\n float v = relu1_shared[relu1_base + c1y * tile_conv1 + c1x];\n float w = w2[((oc * C_out + ic) * 3 + (dy + 1)) * 3 + (dx + 1)];\n sum += v * w;\n }\n }\n }\n sum = sum + b2[oc];\n\n // downsample\n float ds_val = 0.0f;\n int xh = out_h * stride;\n int xw = out_w * stride;\n for (int ic = 0; ic < C_in; ic++) {\n ds_val += x[((bz * C_in + ic) * H + xh) * W + xw] * w_ds[oc * C_in + ic];\n }\n ds_val = ds_val + b_ds[oc];\n\n float res = sum + ds_val;\n if (res < 0.0f) res = 0.0f;\n\n y[((bz * C_out + oc) * H_out + out_h) * W_out + out_w] = res;\n }\n }\n}\n\ntorch::Tensor forward_cuda(\n torch::Tensor x,\n torch::Tensor w1, torch::Tensor b1,\n torch::Tensor w2, torch::Tensor b2,\n torch::Tensor w_ds, torch::Tensor b_ds,\n int stride)\n{\n int B = x.size(0);\n int C_in = x.size(1);\n int H = x.size(2);\n int W = x.size(3);\n int C_out = w1.size(0);\n\n int H_out = (H - 1) / stride + 1;\n int W_out = (W - 1) / stride + 1;\n\n auto y = torch::empty({B, C_out, H_out, W_out}, x.options());\n\n const int TILE = 8;\n dim3 block(256);\n dim3 grid((W_out + TILE - 1) / TILE, (H_out + TILE - 1) / TILE, B);\n\n int tile_conv1 = TILE + 2;\n int tile_in = (tile_conv1 - 1) * stride + 3;\n size_t smem_size = (tile_in * tile_in * C_in + C_out * C_in * 9 + tile_conv1 * tile_conv1 * C_out) * sizeof(float);\n\n fused_basic_block_kernel<<<grid, block, smem_size>>>(\n x.data_ptr<float>(),\n w1.data_ptr<float>(), b1.data_ptr<float>(),\n w2.data_ptr<float>(), b2.data_ptr<float>(),\n w_ds.data_ptr<float>(), b_ds.data_ptr<float>(),\n y.data_ptr<float>(),\n B, C_in, H, W, C_out, stride);\n\n return y;\n}\n\"\"\"\n\ncuda_module = load_inline(\n name=\"resnet_basic_block_cuda_v3\",\n cpp_sources=cpp_sources,\n cuda_sources=cuda_sources,\n functions=[\"forward_cuda\"],\n extra_cuda_cflags=[\"-O3\", \"--use_fast_math\"],\n verbose=False,\n)\n\n\nclass ModelNew(nn.Module):\n expansion = 1\n\n def __init__(self, in_channels, out_channels, stride=1):\n super(ModelNew, self).__init__()\n self.stride = stride\n\n self.conv1 = nn.Conv2d(in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size=3,\n stride=stride, padding=1, bias=False)\n self.bn1 = nn.BatchNorm2d(out_channels)\n self.relu = nn.ReLU(inplace=True)\n self.conv2 = nn.Conv2d(out_channels, out_channels, kernel_size=3,\n stride=1, padding=1, bias=False)\n self.bn2 = nn.BatchNorm2d(out_channels)\n self.downsample = nn.Sequential(\n nn.Conv2d(in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size=1,\n stride=stride, bias=False),\n nn.BatchNorm2d(out_channels),\n )\n\n with torch.no_grad():\n def _fuse(conv, bn):\n w = conv.weight.clone()\n mean = bn.running_mean\n var = bn.running_var\n gamma = bn.weight\n beta = bn.bias\n eps = bn.eps\n scale = gamma / torch.sqrt(var + eps)\n fused_w = w * scale.view(-1, 1, 1, 1)\n fused_b = beta - mean * scale\n return fused_w.contiguous(), fused_b.contiguous()\n\n w1_fused, b1_fused = _fuse(self.conv1, self.bn1)\n w2_fused, b2_fused = _fuse(self.conv2, self.bn2)\n w_ds_fused, b_ds_fused = _fuse(self.downsample[0], self.downsample[1])\n\n self.register_buffer('w1_fused', w1_fused)\n self.register_buffer('b1_fused', b1_fused)\n self.register_buffer('w2_fused', w2_fused)\n self.register_buffer('b2_fused', b2_fused)\n self.register_buffer('w_ds_fused', w_ds_fused)\n self.register_buffer('b_ds_fused', b_ds_fused)\n\n def forward(self, x):\n if self.training:\n identity = x\n out = self.conv1(x)\n out = self.bn1(out)\n out = self.relu(out)\n out = self.conv2(out)\n out = self.bn2(out)\n identity = self.downsample(x)\n out += identity\n out = self.relu(out)\n return out\n\n return cuda_module.forward_cuda(\n x.contiguous(),\n self.w1_fused, self.b1_fused,\n self.w2_fused, self.b2_fused,\n self.w_ds_fused, self.b_ds_fused,\n self.stride,\n )\n" }

Let's see if `load_inline` passes `extra_ldflags` to the final link command. Yes, it does, via `common_cflags` / `extra_ldflags`. In PyTorch's cpp_extension, `extra_ldflags` are appended to the linker command. Let's try this. I'll also add a tiny `cpp_sources` with the forward declaration. If that causes another 'was not declared' error, I might try `cpp_sources=""` again, but maybe the newer torch version handles it better? Hmm. Actually, I recall now: the first error happened because `cpp_sources=""` and the auto-generated main.cpp included `<torch/extension.h>` but `forward_cuda` was not declared. With `cpp_sources` containing the declaration, main.cpp should compile. So I'll use `cpp_sources` with the declaration. Let's write a clean kernel and compile it.

1;\n int base_in_w = base_out_w * stride - 1;\n\n int tid = threadIdx.x;\n\n extern __shared__ float sbuf[];\n float* x_shared = sbuf;\n float* w1_shared = x_shared + tile_in * tile_in * C_in;\n float* relu1_shared = w1_shared + C_out * C_in * 9;\n\n // Load x into shared memory\n int total_in = tile_in * tile_in * C_in;\n for (int idx = tid; idx < total_in; idx += blockDim.x) {\n int c = idx % C_in;\n int rem = idx / C_in;\n int w = rem % tile_in;\n int h = rem / tile_in;\n int gh = base_in_h + h;\n int gw = base_in_w + w;\n float val = 0.0f;\n if (gh >= 0 && gh < H && gw >= 0 && gw < W) {\n val = x[((bz * C_in + c) * H + gh) * W + gw];\n }\n x_shared[(h * tile_in + w) * C_in + c] = val;\n }\n\n // Load w1 into shared memory\n int total_w1 = C_out * C_in * 9;\n for (int idx = tid; idx < total_w1; idx += blockDim.x) {\n w1_shared[idx] = w1[idx];\n }\n __syncthreads();\n\n // Compute conv1 + BN + ReLU for the intermediate tile\n int total_conv1 = tile_conv1 * tile_conv1 * C_out;\n for (int idx = tid; idx < total_conv1; idx += blockDim.x) {\n int oc = idx % C_out;\n int pos = idx / C_out;\n int pw = pos % tile_conv1;\n int ph = pos / tile_conv1;\n\n float sum = 0.0f;\n for (int ic = 0; ic < C_in; ic++) {\n for (int dy = -1; dy <= 1; dy++) {\n for (int dx = -1; dx <= 1; dx++) {\n int ix = 1 + pw * stride + dx;\n int iy = 1 + ph * stride + dy;\n float xv = x_shared[(iy * tile_in + ix) * C_in + ic];\n float wv = w1_shared[((oc * C_in + ic) * 3 + (dy + 1)) * 3 + (dx + 1)];\n sum += xv * wv;\n }\n }\n }\n sum = sum + b1[oc];\n if (sum < 0.0f) sum = 0.0f;\n relu1_shared[oc * tile_conv1_area + ph * tile_conv1 + pw] = sum;\n }\n __syncthreads();\n\n // Compute conv2 + downsample + add + ReLU for output positions\n int H_out = (H - 1) / stride + 1;\n int W_out = (W - 1) / stride + 1;\n\n int lane_id = tid & 31;\n int warp_id = tid >> 5;\n int channel_group = warp_id >> 1;\n int spatial_base = (warp_id & 1) << 5;\n int spatial_idx = spatial_base | lane_id;\n\n int tx = spatial_idx % TILE;\n int ty = spatial_idx / TILE;\n int out_h = base_out_h + ty;\n int out_w = base_out_w + tx;\n\n if (spatial_idx < TILE * TILE && out_h < H_out && out_w < W_out) {\n int channels_per_group = (C_out + 3) / 4;\n int oc_start = channel_group * channels_per_group;\n int oc_end = min(oc_start + channels_per_group, C_out);\n\n for (int oc = oc_start; oc < oc_end; ++oc) {\n float sum = 0.0f;\n for (int ic = 0; ic < C_out; ic++) {\n int relu1_base = ic * tile_conv1_area;\n for (int dy = -1; dy <= 1; dy++) {\n int c1y = ty + 1 + dy;\n for (int dx = -1; dx <= 1; dx++) {\n int c1x = tx + 1 + dx;\n float v = relu1_shared[relu1_base + c1y * tile_conv1 + c1x];\n float w = w2[((oc * C_out + ic) * 3 + (dy + 1)) * 3 + (dx + 1)];\n sum += v * w;\n }\n }\n }\n sum = sum + b2[oc];\n\n // downsample\n float ds_val = 0.0f;\n int xh = out_h * stride;\n int xw = out_w * stride;\n for (int ic = 0; ic < C_in; ic++) {\n ds_val += x[((bz * C_in + ic) * H + xh) * W + xw] * w_ds[oc * C_in + ic];\n }\n ds_val = ds_val + b_ds[oc];\n\n float res = sum + ds_val;\n if (res < 0.0f) res = 0.0f;\n\n y[((bz * C_out + oc) * H_out + out_h) * W_out + out_w] = res;\n }\n }\n}\n\ntorch::Tensor forward_cuda(\n torch::Tensor x,\n torch::Tensor w1, torch::Tensor b1,\n torch::Tensor w2, torch::Tensor b2,\n torch::Tensor w_ds, torch::Tensor b_ds,\n int stride)\n{\n int B = x.size(0);\n int C_in = x.size(1);\n int H = x.size(2);\n int W = x.size(3);\n int C_out = w1.size(0);\n\n int H_out = (H - 1) / stride + 1;\n int W_out = (W - 1) / stride + 1;\n\n auto y = torch::empty({B, C_out, H_out, W_out}, x.options());\n\n const int TILE = 8;\n dim3 block(256);\n dim3 grid((W_out + TILE - 1) / TILE, (H_out + TILE - 1) / TILE, B);\n\n int tile_conv1 = TILE + 2;\n int tile_in = (tile_conv1 - 1) * stride + 3;\n size_t smem_size = (tile_in * tile_in * C_in + C_out * C_in * 9 + tile_conv1 * tile_conv1 * C_out) * sizeof(float);\n\n fused_basic_block_kernel<<<grid, block, smem_size>>>(\n x.data_ptr<float>(),\n w1.data_ptr<float>(), b1.data_ptr<float>(),\n w2.data_ptr<float>(), b2.data_ptr<float>(),\n w_ds.data_ptr<float>(), b_ds.data_ptr<float>(),\n y.data_ptr<float>(),\n B, C_in, H, W, C_out, stride);\n\n return y;\n}\n\"\"\"\n\ncuda_module = load_inline(\n name=\"resnet_basic_block_final\",\n cpp_sources=cpp_sources,\n cuda_sources=cuda_sources,\n functions=[\"forward_cuda\"],\n extra_cflags=[\"-O3\"],\n extra_cuda_cflags=[\"-O3\", \"--use_fast_math\"],\n extra_ldflags=[\"-static-libstdc++\"],\n verbose=False,\n)\n\n\nclass ModelNew(nn.Module):\n expansion = 1\n\n def __init__(self, in_channels, out_channels, stride=1):\n super(ModelNew, self).__init__()\n self.stride = stride\n\n self.conv1 = nn.Conv2d(in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size=3,\n stride=stride, padding=1, bias=False)\n self.bn1 = nn.BatchNorm2d(out_channels)\n self.relu = nn.ReLU(inplace=True)\n self.conv2 = nn.Conv2d(out_channels, out_channels, kernel_size=3,\n stride=1, padding=1, bias=False)\n self.bn2 = nn.BatchNorm2d(out_channels)\n self.downsample = nn.Sequential(\n nn.Conv2d(in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size=1,\n stride=stride, bias=False),\n nn.BatchNorm2d(out_channels),\n )\n\n with torch.no_grad():\n def _fuse(conv, bn):\n w = conv.weight.clone()\n mean = bn.running_mean\n var = bn.running_var\n gamma = bn.weight\n beta = bn.bias\n eps = bn.eps\n scale = gamma / torch.sqrt(var + eps)\n fused_w = w * scale.view(-1, 1, 1, 1)\n fused_b = beta - mean * scale\n return fused_w.contiguous(), fused_b.contiguous()\n\n w1_fused, b1_fused = _fuse(self.conv1, self.bn1)\n w2_fused, b2_fused = _fuse(self.conv2, self.bn2)\n w_ds_fused, b_ds_fused = _fuse(self.downsample[0], self.downsample[1])\n\n self.register_buffer('w1_fused', w1_fused)\n self.register_buffer('b1_fused', b1_fused)\n self.register_buffer('w2_fused', w2_fused)\n self.register_buffer('b2_fused', b2_fused)\n self.register_buffer('w_ds_fused', w_ds_fused)\n self.register_buffer('b_ds_fused', b_ds_fused)\n\n def forward(self, x):\n if self.training:\n identity = x\n out = self.conv1(x)\n out = self.bn1(out)\n out = self.relu(out)\n out = self.conv2(out)\n out = self.bn2(out)\n identity = self.downsample(x)\n out += identity\n out = self.relu(out)\n return out\n\n return cuda_module.forward_cuda(\n x.contiguous(),\n self.w1_fused, self.b1_fused,\n self.w2_fused, self.b2_fused,\n self.w_ds_fused, self.b_ds_fused,\n self.stride,\n )\n" }

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

cpp_sources = """
#include <torch/extension.h>
torch::Tensor forward_cuda(
    torch::Tensor x,
    torch::Tensor w1, torch::Tensor b1,
    torch::Tensor w2, torch::Tensor b2,
    torch::Tensor w_ds, torch::Tensor b_ds,
    int stride);
"""

cuda_sources = """
#include <torch/extension.h>

__global__ void __launch_bounds__(256) fused_basic_block_kernel(
    const float* __restrict__ x,
    const float* __restrict__ w1,
    const float* __restrict__ b1,
    const float* __restrict__ w2,
    const float* __restrict__ b2,
    const float* __restrict__ w_ds,
    const float* __restrict__ b_ds,
    float* __restrict__ y,
    int B, int C_in, int H, int W, int C_out, int stride)
{
    const int TILE = 8;
    const int tile_conv1 = TILE + 2;
    const int tile_in = (tile_conv1 - 1) * stride + 3;
    const int tile_conv1_area = tile_conv1 * tile_conv1;

    int bx = blockIdx.x;
    int by = blockIdx.y;
    int bz = blockIdx.z;

    int base_out_h = by * TILE;
    int base_out_w = bx * TILE;
    int base_in_h = base_out_h * stride - 1;
    int base_in_w = base_out_w * stride - 1;

    int tid = threadIdx.x;

    extern __shared__ float sbuf[];
    float* x_shared = sbuf;
    float* w1_shared = x_shared + tile_in * tile_in * C_in;
    float* relu1_shared = w1_shared + C_out * C_in * 9;

    // Load x into shared memory
    int total_in = tile_in * tile_in * C_in;
    for (int idx = tid; idx < total_in; idx += blockDim.x) {
        int c = idx % C_in;
        int rem = idx / C_in;
        int w = rem % tile_in;
        int h = rem / tile_in;
        int gh = base_in_h + h;
        int gw = base_in_w + w;
        float val = 0.0f;
        if (gh >= 0 && gh < H && gw >= 0 && gw < W) {
            val = x[((bz * C_in + c) * H + gh) * W + gw];
        }
        x_shared[(h * tile_in + w) * C_in + c] = val;
    }

    // Load w1 into shared memory
    int total_w1 = C_out * C_in * 9;
    for (int idx = tid; idx < total_w1; idx += blockDim.x) {
        w1_shared[idx] = w1[idx];
    }
    __syncthreads();

    // Compute conv1 + BN + ReLU for the intermediate tile
    int total_conv1 = tile_conv1 * tile_conv1 * C_out;
    for (int idx = tid; idx < total_conv1; idx += blockDim.x) {
        int oc = idx % C_out;
        int pos = idx / C_out;
        int pw = pos % tile_conv1;
        int ph = pos / tile_conv1;

        float sum = 0.0f;
        for (int ic = 0; ic < C_in; ic++) {
            for (int dy = -1; dy <= 1; dy++) {
                for (int dx = -1; dx <= 1; dx++) {
                    int ix = 1 + pw * stride + dx;
                    int iy = 1 + ph * stride + dy;
                    float xv = x_shared[(iy * tile_in + ix) * C_in + ic];
                    float wv = w1_shared[((oc * C_in + ic) * 3 + (dy + 1)) * 3 + (dx + 1)];
                    sum += xv * wv;
                }
            }
        }
        sum = sum + b1[oc];
        if (sum < 0.0f) sum = 0.0f;
        relu1_shared[oc * tile_conv1_area + ph * tile_conv1 + pw] = sum;
    }
    __syncthreads();

    // Compute conv2 + downsample + add + ReLU for output positions
    int H_out = (H - 1) / stride + 1;
    int W_out = (W - 1) / stride + 1;

    int lane_id = tid & 31;
    int warp_id = tid >> 5;
    int channel_group = warp_id >> 1;
    int spatial_base = (warp_id & 1) << 5;
    int spatial_idx = spatial_base | lane_id;

    int tx = spatial_idx % TILE;
    int ty = spatial_idx / TILE;
    int out_h = base_out_h + ty;
    int out_w = base_out_w + tx;

    if (spatial_idx < TILE * TILE && out_h < H_out && out_w < W_out) {
        int channels_per_group = (C_out + 3) / 4;
        int oc_start = channel_group * channels_per_group;
        int oc_end = min(oc_start + channels_per_group, C_out);

        for (int oc = oc_start; oc < oc_end; ++oc) {
            float sum = 0.0f;
            for (int ic = 0; ic < C_out; ic++) {
                int relu1_base = ic * tile_conv1_area;
                for (int dy = -1; dy <= 1; dy++) {
                    int c1y = ty + 1 + dy;
                    for (int dx = -1; dx <= 1; dx++) {
                        int c1x = tx + 1 + dx;
                        float v = relu1_shared[relu1_base + c1y * tile_conv1 + c1x];
                        float w = w2[((oc * C_out + ic) * 3 + (dy + 1)) * 3 + (dx + 1)];
                        sum += v * w;
                    }
                }
            }
            sum = sum + b2[oc];

            // downsample
            float ds_val = 0.0f;
            int xh = out_h * stride;
            int xw = out_w * stride;
            for (int ic = 0; ic < C_in; ic++) {
                ds_val += x[((bz * C_in + ic) * H + xh) * W + xw] * w_ds[oc * C_in + ic];
            }
            ds_val = ds_val + b_ds[oc];

            float res = sum + ds_val;
            if (res < 0.0f) res = 0.0f;

            y[((bz * C_out + oc) * H_out + out_h) * W_out + out_w] = res;
        }
    }
}

torch::Tensor forward_cuda(
    torch::Tensor x,
    torch::Tensor w1, torch::Tensor b1,
    torch::Tensor w2, torch::Tensor b2,
    torch::Tensor w_ds, torch::Tensor b_ds,
    int stride)
{
    int B = x.size(0);
    int C_in = x.size(1);
    int H = x.size(2);
    int W = x.size(3);
    int C_out = w1.size(0);

    int H_out = (H - 1) / stride + 1;
    int W_out = (W - 1) / stride + 1;

    auto y = torch::empty({B, C_out, H_out, W_out}, x.options());

    const int TILE = 8;
    dim3 block(256);
    dim3 grid((W_out + TILE - 1) / TILE, (H_out + TILE - 1) / TILE, B);

    int tile_conv1 = TILE + 2;
    int tile_in = (tile_conv1 - 1) * stride + 3;
    size_t smem_size = (tile_in * tile_in * C_in + C_out * C_in * 9 + tile_conv1 * tile_conv1 * C_out) * sizeof(float);

    fused_basic_block_kernel<<<grid, block, smem_size>>>(
        x.data_ptr<float>(),
        w1.data_ptr<float>(), b1.data_ptr<float>(),
        w2.data_ptr<float>(), b2.data_ptr<float>(),
        w_ds.data_ptr<float>(), b_ds.data_ptr<float>(),
        y.data_ptr<float>(),
        B, C_in, H, W, C_out, stride);

    return y;
}
"""

cuda_module = load_inline(
    name="resnet_basic_block_final",
    cpp_sources=cpp_sources,
    cuda_sources=cuda_sources,
    functions=["forward_cuda"],
    extra_cflags=["-O3"],
    extra_cuda_cflags=["-O3", "--use_fast_math"],
    extra_ldflags=["-static-libstdc++"],
    verbose=False,
)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    expansion = 1

    def __init__(self, in_channels, out_channels, stride=1):
        super(ModelNew, self).__init__()
        self.stride = stride

        self.conv1 = nn.Conv2d(in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size=3,
                               stride=stride, padding=1, bias=False)
        self.bn1 = nn.BatchNorm2d(out_channels)
        self.relu = nn.ReLU(inplace=True)
        self.conv2 = nn.Conv2d(out_channels, out_channels, kernel_size=3,
                               stride=1, padding=1, bias=False)
        self.bn2 = nn.BatchNorm2d(out_channels)
        self.downsample = nn.Sequential(
            nn.Conv2d(in_channels, out_channels, kernel_size=1,
                      stride=stride, bias=False),
            nn.BatchNorm2d(out_channels),
        )

        with torch.no_grad():
            def _fuse(conv, bn):
                w = conv.weight.clone()
                mean = bn.running_mean
                var = bn.running_var
                gamma = bn.weight
                beta = bn.bias
                eps = bn.eps
                scale = gamma / torch.sqrt(var + eps)
                fused_w = w * scale.view(-1, 1, 1, 1)
                fused_b = beta - mean * scale
                return fused_w.contiguous(), fused_b.contiguous()

            w1_fused, b1_fused = _fuse(self.conv1, self.bn1)
            w2_fused, b2_fused = _fuse(self.conv2, self.bn2)
            w_ds_fused, b_ds_fused = _fuse(self.downsample[0], self.downsample[1])

            self.register_buffer('w1_fused', w1_fused)
            self.register_buffer('b1_fused', b1_fused)
            self.register_buffer('w2_fused', w2_fused)
            self.register_buffer('b2_fused', b2_fused)
            self.register_buffer('w_ds_fused', w_ds_fused)
            self.register_buffer('b_ds_fused', b_ds_fused)

    def forward(self, x):
        if self.training:
            identity = x
            out = self.conv1(x)
            out = self.bn1(out)
            out = self.relu(out)
            out = self.conv2(out)
            out = self.bn2(out)
            identity = self.downsample(x)
            out += identity
            out = self.relu(out)
            return out

        return cuda_module.forward_cuda(
            x.contiguous(),
            self.w1_fused, self.b1_fused,
            self.w2_fused, self.b2_fused,
            self.w_ds_fused, self.b_ds_fused,
            self.stride,
        )
